<div id="review_1266280353" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1266280353" />
    <a title="Angus Killick" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25784798-angus-killick"><img alt="Angus Killick" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1266280353?book_show_action=true">Apr 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angus Killick" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angus Killick" href="/user/show/25784798-angus-killick">Angus Killick</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1266280353" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2173378050750115201">Wow, I read this in one fell swoop and loved every single word! This is such a taught and beautifully crafted piece of writing. A boy and his imaginary friend, Crenshaw, weather the storms of a difficult life at home when his family fall on hard times. Jackson, tries to resist his fantastical friend by denying his 'need' for him, but eventually the relationship finds a place of acceptance and life is easier to bear. Brilliantly written in short economic chapters, with such warmth and gentle humo</span>
  <span id="freeText2173378050750115201" style="display:none">Wow, I read this in one fell swoop and loved every single word! This is such a taught and beautifully crafted piece of writing. A boy and his imaginary friend, Crenshaw, weather the storms of a difficult life at home when his family fall on hard times. Jackson, tries to resist his fantastical friend by denying his 'need' for him, but eventually the relationship finds a place of acceptance and life is easier to bear. Brilliantly written in short economic chapters, with such warmth and gentle humor. I predict this will become an instant classic - it is such a tour-de-force after the wonderful Newbery-winning One and Only Ivan, also penned by Applegate. A real treat is in store when Crenshaw is released into the world. This rises high on my list of all-time favorite middle-grade books instantly! </span>
  <a data-text-id="2173378050750115201" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('E0XSMYwLFBXjrSbKAPZAZCnzjm6HcwP0r6GXw4K7tkFQoDzm7HqrSmbSFLvaH92hM+ttAB+YcBG22q90JphDBQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Ns42af/rl/uD7WN9wXWSYMrDfaAfdHKW+O7mqs/GuQ11K9i+n5oopAaSUQwbnA+l0NuezoefAXPhld4da+VMSQ==')})
  }
//]]>

          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer4984969619713123233">Katherine Applegate is the author of <i>The One and Only Ivan</i>, winner of the 2013 Newbery Medal. Her novel <i>Crenshaw</i> spent over twenty weeks on the <i>New York Times</i> children's bestseller list, and her first middle-grade stand-alone novel, the award-winning <i>Home of the Brave</i>, continues to be included on state reading lists, summer reading lists, and class reading lists.<br/><br/>Katherine has written three picture</span>
  <span id="freeText4984969619713123233" style="display:none">Katherine Applegate is the author of <i>The One and Only Ivan</i>, winner of the 2013 Newbery Medal. Her novel <i>Crenshaw</i> spent over twenty weeks on the <i>New York Times</i> children's bestseller list, and her first middle-grade stand-alone novel, the award-winning <i>Home of the Brave</i>, continues to be included on state reading lists, summer reading lists, and class reading lists.<br /><br />Katherine has written three picture books: <i>The Buffalo Storm</i>; <i>The Remarkable True Story of Ivan, the Shopping Mall Gorilla</i> (often used as a companion book to <i>The One and Only Ivan</i> for younger readers); and <i>Sometimes You Fly</i> (publishing in spring, 2018). For beginning readers, Katherine wrote <i>Roscoe Riley Rules</i>, a seven-book series.<br /><br />With her husband, Michael Grant, Katherine co-wrote <i>Animorphs</i>, a long-running series that has sold over 35 million books worldwide.<br /><br />Katherine lives in Marin County, California, with her family and assorted pets.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4984969619713123233" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
